<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лохмотья.html>лохмо́тья</a> (11315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лохмо́т</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">loxmót</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ья</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ло́хма</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóxma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лохмотья.html>лохмо́тья</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">loxmótʹja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лохмотья.html>лохмо́тьев</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>rags; tatters; duds; frazzles</li></ol>

***лошадиный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадиный.html>лошади́ный</a> (8674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóšadʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадиный.html>лошади́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lošadínyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадиный.html>лошади́ная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lošadínaja</b> síla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horsepower</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лошадь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a> (823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lošadĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*лоша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*loša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">алаша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">alaşa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pack horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuvash_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chuvash language">Chuvash</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="cv">лаша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laša</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">алаша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">alaşa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a kind of camel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crimean_Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Crimean Tatar language">Crimean Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="crh">алаша</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лоск.html>лоск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">losk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dell, hollow, lowland <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лощина.html>лощи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">loščína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лощина.html>лощи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лощина.html>лощи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лощина.html>лощи́н</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лояльность.html>лоя́льность</a> (16978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лужица.html>лу́жица</a> (16618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лужица.html>лу́жица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lúžica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лужица.html>лу́жицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лужица.html>лу́жицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лужица.html>лу́жиц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лужа.html>лу́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (a small) puddle, pool</li></ol>

***лук.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лук</a> (2346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lukъ</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laukaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lauch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">leek</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">laukr</i> whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">løg</i>). Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polabian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polabian language">Polabian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pox">lāuk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">luk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">luk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лук</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">luk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лу́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лу́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лу́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collectively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> onion, onions

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lǫkъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">lankas</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>bow <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">weapon used for shooting arrows</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***лука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лука</a> (29114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lǫka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лука́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">luká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>луки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лу́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лук.html>лук</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bend <i>(in a river or road)</i></li>
<li>pommel <i>(of a saddle)</i></li>
<li>saddlebow</li></ol>

***лукавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лукавить.html>лука́вить</a> (23620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лукавить.html>лука́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lukávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">слука́вить</b>)

***лукавый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лукавый.html>лука́вый</a> (25600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lǫkavъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лукавый.html>лука́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lukávyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sly, crafty, cunning</li>
<li>arch, playful <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">knowing, clever, mischievous</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-лукав-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковица.html>лу́ковица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lúkovica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковица.html>лу́ковицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковица.html>лу́ковицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковица.html>лу́ковиц</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лу́ковичный</b>)

***луковка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:луковка.html>лу́ковка</a> (28120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковка.html>лу́ковка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lúkovka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковка.html>лу́ковки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковка.html>лу́ковки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луковка.html>лу́ковок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>diminutive of</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:луковица.html>лу́ковица</a></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>лу́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ковы.html>ко́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лунатик.html>луна́тик</a> (23749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lunatiker</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sleepwalker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lūnāticus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунатик.html>луна́тик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lunátik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунатик.html>луна́тика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунатик.html>луна́тики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунатик.html>луна́тиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лунати́чка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sleepwalker, somnambulist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lunatic</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>лунь</a> (10441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>лунь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lunʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>луня́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>луни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>луне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">bird</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> harrier, ring-tail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>лунь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болотный.html>боло́тный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lunʹ bolotnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">marsh harrier; duck hawk</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>лунь</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>белый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лунь.html>лунь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sedoj kak lunʹ; belyj kak lunʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">white-haired; white as snow</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лупить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лупить.html>лупи́ть</a> (8115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лупити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lupiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lupiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewp-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to peel, to break off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">labë</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Laub</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">liber</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лупить.html>лупи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to peel, to bark
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:облупить.html>облупи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oblupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to thrash, to flog, to spank, to beat, to batter
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлупить.html>отлупи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to beat, to drub, to clobber
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлупить.html>отлупи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knock, to hit, to zap, to shoot <i>(at)</i>, to fire <i>(on)</i>, to bomb
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">влупи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vlupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лупану́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lupanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fleece (someone) (of a certain amount)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">слупи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

<p><b>лу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c④.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:отлупить.html>отлупи́ть</a>, слупи́ть.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-луп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***луч.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луч</a> (1906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лучь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lučĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lučь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ray; torch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">lowkyo-</i>, which is derived from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewk-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">luč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луча́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>лучи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ray, beam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> radius bone</li></ol>

***лучевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучевой.html>лучево́й</a> (13685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луч</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">luč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучевой.html>лучево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lučevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ray, beam; radial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучевой.html>лучева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:антенна.html>анте́нна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lučevája</b> antɛ́nna</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/beam_antenna" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:beam antenna"><b>beam</b> antenna</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучевой.html>лучева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>кость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lučevája</b> kostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">radius <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the forearm</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>radial</b> bone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> radiation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лучевой.html>лучева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lučevája</b> boléznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>radiation</b> sickness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучина.html>лучи́на</a> (17417)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучина.html>лучи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lučína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучина.html>лучи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучина.html>лучи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучина.html>лучи́н</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучинка.html>лучи́нка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>splinter, chip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a small torch made of a single splinter</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
